<div class="col-lg-11 row block2-wrapper">
<div class="col-lg-6 offset-lg-1">
<h2 class="slide" data-side="text-up">
Onze nieuwsmerken                    </h2>
<div class="my-3 slide" data-side="text-up2">
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">BDUmedia is al 154 jaar dé specialist in lokaal bereik. In 1871 begonnen met lokale nieuwsbrengers en inmiddels uitgegroeid tot marktleider in lokale nieuwsmedia. Met tal van <a href="https://bdumedia.nl/nieuwsmerk/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">kranten, magazines en onlineplatforms</a> bereiken we wekelijks miljoenen Nederlanders, óók bij jou in de buurt. </span></p>
</div>
<a class="btn btn-primary me-2 slide" data-side="text-up3" href="/organisatie/">Over ons</a>
<a class="btn btn-outline-secondary slide" data-side="text-up3" href="/nieuwsmerken/">Nieuwsmerken</a>
</div>

function updateMapStyle(){
const map=document.querySelector('.kaart1 svg');
popupholder= document.querySelector('.kaart-popup-holders');
popupholder.style.height=map.clientHeight+'px';
popupholder.style.width=map.clientWidth+'px';
const markers=document.querySelectorAll('.kaart-popup');
markers.forEach(marker=>{
const target=document.querySelector('#'+marker.getAttribute('data-target'));
const popup=document.querySelector('#popup-'+marker.getAttribute('data-target'));
const markerSpot=target.querySelector('rect');
const targetrect=markerSpot.getBoundingClientRect();
let maprect=map.getBoundingClientRect();
let markerrect=marker.getBoundingClientRect();
popup.style.top=(targetrect.top-maprect.top)-40+'px';
popup.style.left=(targetrect.left-maprect.left)+12+'px';
});
}
updateMapStyle();
window.addEventListener('resize', updateMapStyle);
document.querySelectorAll(".regio-clicker").forEach(marker=>{
marker.addEventListener("click", function(e){
marker.classList.toggle('active');
e.preventDefault();
document.querySelectorAll(".kaart-popup").forEach(popup=>
{
if(popup.id!="popup-"+marker.id){
popup.classList.remove('active');
}
});
const popup=document.querySelector('#popup-'+marker.id);
popup.style.setProperty('--height',(popup.scrollHeight+40)+'px');
popup.classList.toggle('active');
});
});
document.querySelectorAll(".kaart-popup").forEach(popup=>{
popup.style.width= popup.clientWidth+ 20+ "px"
})
document.addEventListener("click",e=>{
if((e.target.classList.contains("kaart-popup") || e.target.classList.contains('.regio-clicker') || e.target.closest('.kaart-popup') || e.target.closest('.regio-clicker')) && !e.target.matches('.close')){
return;
}
document.querySelectorAll(".kaart-popup,.regio-clicker").forEach(popup=>{
popup.classList.remove('active');
});
})
</script>
</div>
